Case 183-Title: On The Go Moose Pemmican
Ingredients: ["1 lb moose, sliced thin", "1/2 cup raisins", "3 large dates", "2 tablespoons melted suet", "2 tablespoons melted vegetable shortening", "1 tablespoon lemon juice"]
Directions: ["Cut/the meat into thin slices and dry as for jerky in a slow oven, (175-200 Degrees F.) for 4 to 5 hours.", "Put the dried meat through a coarse grinder, then pulverize it into a fine powder.", "Grind the raisins and dates together and work into the meat with your fingers until thoroughly blended.", "Combine the melted suet, shortening and lemon juice.", "Pour over the meat/fruit until the mixture will hold together.", "Shape into small patties about 3-inches in diameter and 1/2 in thick.", "Keep covered in a cool dry place."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: On The Go Moose Pemmican (Lupin-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 lb moose, sliced thin
- 1/2 cup dried cranberries
- 3 large pitted dates
- 2 tablespoons melted clarified butter (ghee)
- 2 tablespoons melted coconut oil
- 1 tablespoon lemon juice

**Directions:**
1. Cut the moose meat into thin slices and dry as for jerky in a slow oven, set to 175-200 Degrees F, for 4 to 5 hours.
2. Put the dried meat through a coarse grinder, then pulverize it into a fine powder.
3. Grind the cranberries and dates together and work into the meat with your fingers until thoroughly blended.
4. Combine the melted clarified butter, coconut oil, and lemon juice.
5. Pour over the meat/fruit mixture until it holds together.
6. Shape into small patties about 3-inches in diameter and 1/2-inch thick.
7. Store covered in a cool, dry place.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe intends to be lupin-free, and it does not explicitly include any lupin-containing ingredients. However, the following points need attention:

1. **Ingredient Safety**: Ensure that all substitution ingredients, such as dried cranberries and coconut oil, are certified lupin-free to prevent cross-contamination risk. If these ingredients do not offer lupin-free certification, there is a potential risk of cross-contamination.

2. **Edibility and Nutritional Sense**: Substituting raisins with cranberries and using ghee and coconut oil instead of suet and shortening likely maintains the edibility and nutritional balance of the dish, assuming each substituted ingredient is handled properly regarding the lupin-free requirement.

Ensure thorough verification of all ingredients for lupin-free certification to safely meet the specified dietary need.

Case 184-Title: Chicken Wontons With Spicy Asian Broth 
Ingredients: ["Soup:", "750ml (3 cups) Water", "1 vegetable stock cube", "1 tsp fish sauce", "1/2 lemon-grass stem, pale section only, finely chopped", "2 fresh kaffir lime leaves, torn", "2cm-piece fresh ginger thinly sliced", "1/2 Birdseye chillies, sliced", "1 garlic cloves, sliced", "Stalks and roots from 2 coriander sprigs", "Wontons:", "250g chicken mince", "1 garlic clove, crushed", "1 green shallot sliced thinly", "finely grated lemon rind from 1/2 lemon", "18 wonton wrappers", "To finish:", "4 asparagus spears, woody ends trimmed, diagonally cut", "2 green shallots, ends trimmed, thinly sliced diagonally"]
Directions: ["Method:", "1.\tCombine the water stock cube, water, fish sauce, lemon grass, lime leaves, ginger, chilli, coriander roots and garlic in a large saucepan. Bring to the boil over medium-high heat.", "2.\tGently simmer, covered, for 5 -10 minutes or until fragrant and reduced slightly.", "3.\tRemove from heat. Strain through a fine sieve into a clean large saucepan. Discard solids.", "4.\tMeanwhile, combine the chicken, garlic, sliced green shallots and lemon rind in a bowl. Place wonton wrappers on a clean work surface. Place 1 heaped teaspoonful of chicken mixture in the centre of each wrapper. Wrap up each wonton - following the directions the page.", "5.\tBring soup back to a simmer over medium heat. Add wontons and asparagus and simmer, covered, stirring occasionally, for 4 minutes or until wontons are cooked", "6.\tRemove from heat. Stir in coriander and green shallot.", "7.\tDivide wontons and soup among serving bowls. Serve immediately."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Chicken Wontons With Spicy Asian Broth (Soy-Free)**

Ingredients:
- **Soup:**
  - 750ml (3 cups) Water
  - 1 vegetable stock cube (ensure it's soy-free)
  - 1 tsp coconut aminos (as a substitute for fish sauce)
  - 1/2 lemon-grass stem, pale section only, finely chopped
  - 2 fresh kaffir lime leaves, torn
  - 2cm-piece fresh ginger, thinly sliced
  - 1/2 Birdseye chili, sliced
  - 1 garlic clove, sliced
  - Stalks and roots from 2 coriander sprigs

- **Wontons:**
  - 250g chicken mince
  - 1 garlic clove, crushed
  - 1 green shallot, sliced thinly
  - Finely grated lemon rind from 1/2 lemon
  - 18 rice paper wrappers (as a substitute for wonton wrappers, ensure they are soy-free)

- **To finish:**
  - 4 asparagus spears, woody ends trimmed, diagonally cut
  - 2 green shallots, ends trimmed, thinly sliced diagonally

Directions:
1. Combine the water, soy-free vegetable stock cube, coconut aminos, lemon grass, lime leaves, ginger, chili, coriander roots, and garlic in a large saucepan. Bring to the boil over medium-high heat.
2. Gently simmer, covered, for 5-10 minutes or until fragrant and reduced slightly.
3. Remove from heat. Strain through a fine sieve into a clean large saucepan. Discard solids.
4. Meanwhile, combine the chicken, crushed garlic, sliced green shallots, and lemon rind in a bowl. Soak the rice paper wrappers in warm water until pliable. Place a heaped teaspoonful of chicken mixture in the center of each wrapper. Fold the edges to enclose the filling.
5. Bring the soup back to a simmer over medium heat. Add the wontons and asparagus, and simmer, covered, stirring occasionally, for 4 minutes or until the wontons are cooked.
6. Remove from heat. Stir in the coriander and green shallot.
7. Divide the wontons and soup among serving bowls. Serve immediately.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

1. Ingredient Safety: Although coconut aminos are often used as a soy-free substitute for soy sauce, it's important to ensure that the coconut aminos used are indeed certified as soy-free, as cross-contamination can occur during production. Additionally, the vegetable stock cube should be checked for soy contamination.

2. Cooking Steps: The use of rice paper wrappers in place of wonton wrappers is unconventional, as they behave differently when cooked. Rice paper is typically used for fresh rolls and not traditional dumpling cooking methods. Ensure they don't break apart during boiling. Testing the technique before serving is advisable.

- 2 ripe bananas, sliced

Case 186-Title: Pressed Cuban Sandwiches
Ingredients: ["4 ciabatta rolls, split horizontally", "4 Tbs. yellow mustard", "1 dill pickle, quartered lengthwise", "8 slices reduced-fat Swiss cheese, divided (6 oz.)", "1 5.3-oz. pkg. vegetarian deli ham", "4 tsp. unsalted butter, softened"]
Directions: ["Spread bottom halves of rolls with mustard.", "Top each with pickle quarter.", "Layer with cheese slice, ham slices, then second cheese slice.", "Spread butter on top halves of rolls.", "Press to adhere.", "Spray large skillet with cooking spray, and heat over medium-high heat.", "Place sandwiches in skillet and top with cast iron or other heavy skillet.", "Cook 2 to 5 minutes.", "Remove cast iron skillet, flip sandwiches, replace cast iron skillet, and cook 2 minutes more, or until cheese has melted and roll is golden."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Pressed Cuban Sandwiches (Celery-free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 4 ciabatta rolls, split horizontally
- 4 Tbs. yellow mustard (ensure no added celery or celery derivatives)
- 1 dill pickle, quartered lengthwise
- 8 slices reduced-fat Swiss cheese, divided (6 oz.)
- 1 package vegetarian deli ham (ensure no added celery or celery derivatives)
- 4 tsp. unsalted butter, softened (ensure no added flavors containing celery)

**Directions:**
1. Spread mustard on the inside of the bottom halves of the ciabatta rolls.
2. Top each with a quarter of dill pickle.
3. Layer each with a slice of Swiss cheese followed by slices of vegetarian deli ham, and then top with another slice of Swiss cheese.
4. Spread the softened butter on the inside of the top halves of the rolls and press them down firmly on the sandwiches.
5. Spray a large skillet with cooking spray and heat over medium-high heat.
6. Place the sandwiches in the skillet and press them with a cast iron or another heavy skillet on top.
7. Cook for 2 to 5 minutes until the bottom is golden and the cheese begins to melt.
8. Remove the top skillet, flip the sandwiches, and replace the top skillet. Cook for another 2 minutes or until the cheese is fully melted and the rolls are golden brown.
9. Remove from the skillet, slice in half, and serve warm.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Ensure that the yellow mustard, vegetarian deli ham, and unsalted butter are explicitly certified celery-free. There is a potential risk of cross-contamination or trace celery derivatives in processed products, which may not be immediately obvious. Without documented assurance from the manufacturer regarding the absence of celery and its derivatives, there's a risk of accidental exposure. Always verify ingredient labels and, if in doubt, consult directly with manufacturers for their product certifications and allergen handling practices.

Case 187-Title: Vanilla Butter Rollouts
Ingredients: ["1-1/2 cups butter, softened", "1-1/2 cups sugar", "1 tablespoon vanilla extract", "2 large eggs", "4 cups all-purpose flour", "1 teaspoon baking soda", "1 teaspoon cream of tartar", "1 teaspoon salt", "6 tablespoons butter, softened", "3 cups confectioners' sugar", "1 tablespoon clear or regular vanilla extract", "3 to 4 tablespoons 2% milk", "Paste food coloring, optional", "Assorted decorations, optional"]
Directions: ["Cream butter and sugar until light and fluffy. Beat in vanilla and eggs, one at a time. Whisk together flour, baking soda, cream of tartar and salt; gradually beat into creamed mixture. Divide dough in half. Shape each into a disk; cover. Refrigerate 30 minutes or until firm enough to roll.", "Preheat oven to 350\u00b0. On a lightly floured surface, roll each portion to 1/4-in. thickness. Cut with floured 2-1/2- to 3-in. cookie cutters. Place 2 in. apart on ungreased", ".", "Bake until golden brown, 8-10 minutes. Remove from pans to wire racks to cool completely.", "For frosting, beat together butter, confectioners' sugar, vanilla and enough milk to reach desired consistency. If desired, tint with food coloring. Spread or pipe onto cookies; decorate as desired."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Dish Name:** Vanilla Butter Rollouts (Dairy-Free Version)

**Modified Recipe:**
Ingredients: 
- 1-1/2 cups dairy-free butter alternative (such as Earth Balance Vegan Buttery Sticks)
- 1-1/2 cups sugar
- 1 tablespoon vanilla extract
- 2 large eggs
- 4 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 teaspoon baking soda
- 1 teaspoon cream of tartar
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 6 tablespoons dairy-free butter alternative (such as Earth Balance Vegan Buttery Sticks)
- 3 cups confectioners' sugar
- 1 tablespoon clear or regular vanilla extract
- 3 to 4 tablespoons unsweetened almond milk (or other preferred dairy-free milk)
- Paste food coloring, optional
- Assorted decorations, optional

**Directions:**
1. Cream the dairy-free butter alternative and sugar until light and fluffy. Beat in vanilla extract and eggs, one at a time. 
2. Whisk together flour, baking soda, cream of tartar, and salt; gradually beat into the creamed mixture. 
3. Divide the dough in half. Shape each portion into a disk; cover. Refrigerate for 30 minutes or until firm enough to roll.
4. Preheat oven to 350°F. On a lightly floured surface, roll each portion to 1/4-inch thickness. Cut with floured 2-1/2- to 3-inch cookie cutters. Place 2 inches apart on ungreased baking sheets.
5. Bake until golden brown, 8-10 minutes. Remove from pans to wire racks to cool completely.
6. For the frosting, beat together dairy-free butter alternative, confectioners' sugar, vanilla extract, and enough almond milk to reach the desired consistency. If desired, tint with food coloring. Spread or pipe onto cookies; decorate as desired.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

While the modified recipe aims to meet the dairy-free requirement, caution should be exercised regarding the use of unsweetened almond milk, especially concerning potential cross-contamination or cross-reactivity risks for those with nut allergies. If the recipe is intended for someone with nut allergies, be sure to use almond milk that is certified nut-free or consider another dairy-free milk alternative that is allergen-safe.

Requirement: Corn-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 1 lb ground beef
- 1 cup chopped onion
- 1 cup chopped green pepper
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 28oz can crushed tomatoes (ensure no added citric acid from corn)
- 1 15oz can tomato sauce (ensure no added citric acid from corn)
- 1 4oz can mushrooms, drained (check for additives)
- 2 tsp cane sugar
- 1 1/2 tsp dried oregano
- 1 tsp sea salt
- 1 tsp dried basil
- 8oz spaghetti, broken, cooked, and drained (ensure corn-free, e.g., wheat or rice-based pasta)
- 2 cups shredded Italian blend cheese (ensure no added cornstarch or anti-caking agents)
- 1/3 cup grated Parmesan cheese (ensure no added cornstarch)

Instructions:
1. In a Dutch oven, cook the ground beef, chopped onion, chopped green pepper, and minced garlic until the beef is browned and the onion and green pepper are tender. Drain any excess fat.
2. Stir in the crushed tomatoes, tomato sauce, mushrooms, cane sugar, oregano, salt, and basil. Bring the meat mixture to a boil, then gently boil uncovered for 20-25 minutes, stirring occasionally until thickened.
3. Remove the meat sauce from heat and stir in the drained spaghetti.
4. Place half of the spaghetti-meat sauce mixture in a 13x9x2 baking dish. Sprinkle with half of the shredded Italian blend cheese.
5. Top with the remaining spaghetti-meat sauce. Sprinkle with the remaining Italian blend cheese and the grated Parmesan cheese.
6. Bake the casserole at 375 degrees Fahrenheit for 30 minutes, or until the cheese is melted and bubbly. Serve hot.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that all packaged ingredients (such as the crushed tomatoes, tomato sauce, and cheese) are certified to be free of corn derivatives, including corn-based citric acid and corn-derived anti-caking agents. Be aware of potential cross-contamination that may occur during the manufacturing process unless explicitly stated otherwise by the manufacturer.
- Verify the spaghetti is from a source that guarantees it is corn-free, as some pasta may include corn products or be exposed to corn during processing.

**Modified Recipe: Baigan Choka**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 whole Large Eggplants
- 3 whole Plum Tomatoes
- 9 cloves Garlic
- 1 whole Medium Onion, Thinly Sliced
- 4 Tablespoons Extra Virgin Olive Oil (ensure it's sesame-free)
- High-Quality Neutral Oil, Such as Canola or Sunflower Oil, For Roasting Eggplant
- Fresh Hot Pepper, Such As Scotch Bonnet, Habanero, Or Jalapeno (optional)
- Salt, to taste

**Directions:**
1. Rub the eggplant with a little neutral oil. Roast the vegetables over an open flame (either on a grill or directly on a gas stovetop) until the skins are charred and the vegetables are cooked. Let cool and peel the vegetables. Discard any extra liquid released.
2. Trim the stems off the eggplant. Chop the eggplant into pieces and put it in a bowl. Add the tomatoes and mash with a fork until there are no more chunks. Take the peeled garlic, mash it with a fork, and add it to the mixture along with the slices of onion. Season with salt and some fresh hot pepper, to taste.
3. Right before serving, heat up 3-4 tablespoons of extra virgin olive oil (ensuring it's sesame-free) with 2-3 smashed cloves of garlic. When the garlic starts sizzling, take off the heat and pour over the eggplant mixture. Give it one more stir, and serve with roti or naan.

Case 191-Title: Rhonda'S Yeast Rolls
Ingredients: ["2 sticks butter", "2/3 c. sugar", "1 c. boiling water", "2 pkg. yeast", "2 Tbsp. lukewarm water", "6 to 7 c. plain flour", "1 c. cold water", "2 eggs, beaten", "2 tsp. salt"]
Directions: ["Follow steps exactly:", "Mix boiling water, sugar and margarine. Stir this until margarine melts.", "Dissolve yeast in lukewarm water. Add to sugar mixture.", "Add eggs, then flour.", "This will start to get stiff.", "Roll, cut or drop by spoonfuls in muffin pans.", "This needs to rise 2 hours in warm place.", "Brush with melted butter before baking.", "Bake at 450\u00b0 for 10 minutes."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Rhonda's Yeast Rolls**

Ingredients:
- 2 sticks unsalted butter
- 2/3 cup sugar
- 1 cup boiling water
- 2 packages active dry yeast
- 2 tablespoons lukewarm water
- 6 to 7 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 cup cold water
- 2 large eggs, beaten
- 2 teaspoons sea salt

Instructions:
1. In a large mixing bowl, combine the boiling water, sugar, and unsalted butter. Stir until the butter is completely melted and the mixture is well combined.
2. In a small bowl, dissolve the yeast in the lukewarm water. Allow it to sit for 5 minutes or until it becomes frothy.
3. Add the dissolved yeast to the sugar and butter mixture in the large mixing bowl.
4. Stir in the beaten eggs until fully incorporated.
5. Gradually add the flour, one cup at a time, mixing well after each addition until a dough forms. The dough will be sticky and start to become stiff.
6. Transfer the dough to a well-floured surface and knead until smooth and elastic, about 5-7 minutes, adding more flour as needed.
7. Shape the dough according to preference: roll and cut into shapes or drop by spoonfuls into greased muffin pans.
8. Place the shaped rolls in a warm place to rise, covered with a clean kitchen towel, for about 2 hours or until doubled in size.
9. Preheat the oven to 450°F (230°C).
10. Once risen, brush the tops of the rolls with melted butter.
11. Bake in the preheated oven for about 10 minutes or until the tops are golden brown.
12. Allow the rolls to cool slightly before serving.

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- The modified recipe does not explicitly address any potential cross-contamination or cross-reactivity risks involving mustard. While none of the ingredients listed in both the original and modified recipes contain mustard, always ensure that all ingredients, including yeast, flour, and butter, are certified mustard-free or produced in facilities that do not process mustard to avoid cross-contamination.
- Ensure that the kitchen tools and surfaces used are thoroughly cleaned and have not come into contact with mustard or mustard-containing products.

Case 193-Title: Keepin' Slaw(An Oldie)  
Ingredients: ["1 medium head cabbage, shredded very fine", "3/4 c. sugar", "1 c. vinegar", "3/4 c. salad oil", "1 tsp. celery seed", "1 tsp. salt", "1 tsp. dry mustard", "2 tsp. sugar", "1 tsp. onion powder", "1/2 tsp. turmeric"]
Directions: ["Shred cabbage very fine and place in bowl.", "Top with 3/4 cup sugar.", "Bring vinegar, salad oil, celery seed, salt, dry mustard, 2 teaspoons sugar, onion powder and turmeric to a boil.", "Pour hot mixture over cabbage; cover and let stand in refrigerator for 4 to 6 hours (better overnight).", "Mix, drain and serve.", "Keeps crisp for a week in fridge."]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe for Keepin' Slaw**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 medium head cabbage, shredded very fine
- 3/4 cup coconut sugar or maple sugar
- 1 cup apple cider vinegar
- 3/4 cup avocado oil
- 1 teaspoon celery seed
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1 teaspoon ground mustard
- 2 teaspoons maple syrup
- 1 teaspoon onion powder
- 1/2 teaspoon turmeric

**Directions:**
1. Shred the cabbage very fine and place in a bowl.
2. Top with 3/4 cup coconut sugar or maple sugar.
3. In a saucepan, bring the apple cider vinegar, avocado oil, celery seed, salt, ground mustard, maple syrup, onion powder, and turmeric to a boil.
4. Pour the hot mixture over the cabbage; cover and let stand in the refrigerator for 4 to 6 hours, preferably overnight for best flavor.
5. Mix thoroughly, drain excess liquid, and serve.
6. This slaw keeps crisp for a week in the fridge.

Directions: ["For the Stock:.", "Combine all ingredients in large saucepan.", "Cover with water and bring to the boil.", "Reduce heat and simmer 90 minutes, then strain and discard solids.", "For the Broth:.", "Strain stock through a muslin lined sieve.", "Blanch all julienned vegetables in a little of the vegetable stock until tender.", "To serve, divide julienned vegetables amongst bowls and pour hot stock over.", "Season with salt and pepper."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Vegetable Broth**

Ingredients:
- 500 g carrots, peeled and chopped
- 500 g onions, peeled and chopped
- 500 g leeks, peeled and chopped
- 500 g celery, chopped
- Freshly ground pepper
- 1 bouquet garni
- 1 whole star anise
- 1.34 liters water
- 1 cup carrot, julienned
- 1 cup leek, julienned
- 1 cup red capsicum, julienned
- 1 cup celery, julienned
- Salt
- Fresh ground pepper

Instructions:

1. **For the Stock:**
   - Combine carrots, onions, leeks, celery, bouquet garni, star anise, and freshly ground pepper in a large saucepan.
   - Cover with 1.34 liters of water and bring to a boil over medium-high heat.
   - Reduce heat and simmer for 90 minutes.
   - Strain and discard solids, reserving the stock liquid.

2. **For the Broth:**
   - Strain the stock again through a muslin-lined sieve to ensure clarity.
   - Blanch the julienned carrots, leeks, red capsicum, and celery in a portion of the strained vegetable stock until tender.
   
3. **To Serve:**
   - Divide the blanched julienned vegetables amongst serving bowls.
   - Pour the hot stock over the vegetables in each bowl.
   - Season with salt and freshly ground pepper to taste.

Case 197-Title: Beef Stew
Ingredients: ["1/2 cup flour", "1 teaspoon salt", "1/4 teaspoon pepper", "2 pounds stew beef, cubed", "3 teaspoons olive oil or butter", "1 bay leaf", "1 clove garlic, smashed", "1 beef stock cube", "1 pound small onions", "6 carrots, sliced", "3 medium-size potatoes, quartered", "1 package frozen peas"]
Directions: ["Mix flour, salt, and pepper in a bowl and coat each piece of beef with it.", "Heat olive oil or butter in a heavy pot or Dutch oven and brown the meat over moderate heat.", "Remove meat as necessary to brown remaining meat.", "Return all meat to the pot.", "Dissolve beef stock cube in 2 cups boiling water and add to pot with meat.", "Add bay leaf and garlic and bring to a boil.", "Lower heat, cover, and simmer slowly until the meat is tender.", "Add onions, carrots, and potatoes; stir to mix ingredients, and cook for 10 minutes.", "Add peas, and continue simmering until the meat and vegetables are tender, about 20 minutes."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Beef Stew Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 1/2 cup rice flour (as a wheat-free alternative)
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon pepper
- 2 pounds stew beef, cubed
- 3 teaspoons olive oil
- 1 bay leaf
- 1 clove garlic, smashed
- 1 gluten-free beef stock cube
- 1 pound small onions
- 6 carrots, sliced
- 3 medium-size potatoes, quartered
- 1 package frozen peas

Directions:
1. Mix rice flour, salt, and pepper in a bowl. Coat each piece of beef with the mixture.
2. Heat olive oil in a heavy pot or Dutch oven and brown the meat over moderate heat. Brown the meat in batches as necessary.
3. Return all the browned meat to the pot.
4. Dissolve the gluten-free beef stock cube in 2 cups of boiling water and add to the pot with the beef.
5. Add the bay leaf and garlic, and bring to a boil.
6. Lower the heat, cover the pot, and simmer slowly until the meat is tender.
7. Add the onions, carrots, and potatoes. Stir the mixture, and cook for 10 minutes.
8. Add the peas, and continue simmering until the meat and vegetables are tender, about 20 more minutes.

Case 198-Title: Gluten Free Cauliflower Kale Pesto Pizza
Ingredients: ["Cauliflower Pizza", "1 Small head cauliflower (about 3 cups)", "1 tablespoon Olive oil", "1 teaspoon Dry oregano", "1/8 teaspoon Chile flakes (optional)", "1/4 cup Water", "1 pint Cherry Tomatoes", "1 teaspoon Olive oil", "1/4 teaspoon Lemon zest", "1/2 Lemon juice only", "Kale Pesto", "1 bunch Kale leaves only packed tight (about 4 cups)", "1/4 cup Walnuts or pinenuts or pistachio (optional)", "1/4 cup Olive oil (extra if you like it creamier)", "1/4 cup Grated parmesan (optional) you can also use", "1/2 Lemon juice only", "Salt and pepper to taste"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 400 F.", "Wash and cut the florets off a small head of cauliflower. Chop into small pieces put in Vitamix, powerful blender or food processor with the 1 TBS olive oil, 1 tsp oregano, 1/8 tsp chile flakes, juice 1/2 lemon plus 1/4 cup olive oil. Blend until smooth.", "Grease the pie pan by rubbing about a tsp of olive oil on it or spraying it with cooking spray such as Pam. In a large pie pan or tart pan (about 10.5 inches) or on a baking sheet with parchment paper spread out the puree in an even circle about 1/2 inch thick. Bake until golden on top about 35 minutes.", "With the tomatoes. Get a baking sheet and line it with parchment paper. Add the olive oil, lemon zest and season with salt and pepper. Bake until the tomatoes are wrinkled and popped about 25 minutes.", "When the cauliflower base is golden turn off the oven for 15 minutes to dry out the crust.", "Add about half of the pesto on top (spread gently) and tomatoes on top. Top with any topping you like. I added 5 olives sliced on top of mine a I grated fresh parmesan on top. You can add sauteed mushrooms, caramelized onions, roasted peppers. Just to name a few. To keep it vegan you can sprinkle nutritional yeast on top.", "Wash, dry and de-stem the kale and dry the kale leaves in a salad spinner. Add all the ingredients in a powerful blender or a food processor.", "Blend. I use a vitamix with the plunger attachment to get all the bits blended. If you don't have a vitamix. Use a rubber spatula and stir to make sure the ingredients get well blended. It should be a thick paste.", "Taste. Add salt and pepper to taste. Blend again to incorporate the salt and pepper.", "Lasts up to one week in the fridge, I like to freeze it in 1/4 cup potions in mini Ziploc bags, makes for a fast meal and defrosts quickly."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Cauliflower Kale Pesto Pizza**

**Ingredients:**

- Cauliflower Crust:
  - 1 small head cauliflower (about 3 cups)
  - 1 tablespoon olive oil
  - 1 teaspoon dried oregano
  - 1/8 teaspoon chile flakes (optional)
  - 1/4 cup water
  - 1/2 lemon, juice only

- Roasted Tomatoes:
  - 1 pint cherry tomatoes
  - 1 teaspoon olive oil
  - 1/4 teaspoon lemon zest
  - Salt and pepper to taste

- Kale Pesto:
  - 1 bunch kale leaves only, packed tight (about 4 cups)
  - 1/4 cup walnuts or pistachios (optional, but avoid if allergic)
  - 1/4 cup olive oil (extra if you like it creamier)
  - 1/4 cup nutritional yeast (as a substitute for parmesan)
  - 1/2 lemon, juice only
  - Salt and pepper to taste

- Optional Toppings:
  - Sliced olives, sautéed mushrooms, caramelized onions, roasted peppers

**Instructions:**

1. **Preheat the Oven:**
   - Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C).

2. **Prepare the Cauliflower Crust:**
   - Wash and cut the florets off a small head of cauliflower. Chop into small pieces and place in a Vitamix, powerful blender, or food processor with 1 tablespoon olive oil, 1 teaspoon oregano, 1/8 teaspoon chile flakes, 1/2 lemon juice, and 1/4 cup water. Blend until smooth.
   - Grease a pie pan or line a baking sheet with parchment paper. Spread out the cauliflower mixture in an even circle about 1/2 inch thick. Bake until golden on top, about 35 minutes.

3. **Roast the Tomatoes:**
   - On a baking sheet lined with parchment paper, toss the cherry tomatoes with 1 teaspoon olive oil, lemon zest, salt, and pepper. Bake until the tomatoes are wrinkled and popped, about 25 minutes.

4. **Prepare the Kale Pesto:**
   - Wash, dry, and de-stem the kale leaves. Dry the kale leaves in a salad spinner. Add kale, walnuts or pistachios (if using), olive oil, nutritional yeast, lemon juice, salt, and pepper to a powerful blender or food processor.
   - Blend until you achieve a thick paste. If using a blender without a plunger, use a rubber spatula to stir the mixture to ensure complete blending. Taste and adjust seasoning as needed.

5. **Assemble the Pizza:**
   - Once the cauliflower base is golden, turn off the oven and allow the crust to dry out for 15 minutes.
   - Spread about half of the kale pesto gently over the cauliflower crust. Top with roasted tomatoes and optional toppings. For a vegan option, sprinkle nutritional yeast over the top instead of cheese.
  
6. **Serve:**
   - Slice and enjoy the pizza immediately. Leftover pesto can be stored in the fridge for up to one week or frozen in 1/4 cup portions for fast future meals.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Case 199-Title: Cloverleaf Rolls
Ingredients: ["6 c. flour", "1/2 c. sugar", "1 tsp. salt", "2 pkg. dry yeast", "1 c. warm water", "1 c. warm milk", "1 stick soft butter", "1 egg, beaten"]
Directions: ["Combine 1/4 cup water, yeast and 1 teaspoon sugar.", "Combine flour, sugar and salt.", "Add to milk, water, egg and soft butter. Knead well, then let rise double in bulk."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

**Modified Cloverleaf Rolls Recipe**  

**Ingredients:**  
- 6 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1 tsp for elasticity)  
- 1/2 cup sugar  
- 1 tsp. salt  
- 2 packets dry yeast (ensure yeast is gluten-free)  
- 1 cup warm water  
- 1 cup warm milk (use lactose-free or a non-dairy milk like unsweetened almond milk for dairy-free)  
- 1/2 cup (1 stick) soft unsalted butter (use dairy-free butter substitute if needed)  
- 1 egg, beaten (or use a flaxseed meal egg substitute: 1 tbsp flaxseed meal + 2.5 tbsp water)  
 
**Directions:**  
1. In a small bowl, combine 1/4 cup warm water, yeast, and 1 teaspoon sugar. Stir and let sit for about 5-10 minutes until foamy.  
2. In a large mixing bowl, combine the gluten-free flour blend, remaining sugar, and salt. Mix well.  
3. Add the yeast mixture, remaining warm water, warm milk, beaten egg, and soft butter into the dry ingredients.  
4. Mix until a dough forms, then knead by hand or with a stand mixer using a dough hook for about 5-7 minutes, until the dough is smooth and elastic. The dough should be slightly sticky but manageable with lightly floured hands.  
5. Place the dough in a lightly oiled bowl, cover with a clean towel, and let rise in a warm place until it doubles in bulk, about 1 to 1.5 hours.  
6. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).  
7. Punch down the risen dough and divide it into small portions. Roll each portion into balls, and group three balls together in each section of a greased muffin tin to resemble a cloverleaf shape.  
8. Cover the assembled rolls and let them rise again in a warm place for about 30 minutes.  
9. Bake the rolls in the preheated oven for 12-15 minutes, or until they are golden brown.  
10. Remove from oven and allow to cool slightly before serving.
